Do furloughed federal employees get back pay?		That is up to the House, Senate &amp; White House. In 2013, furloughed employees received back-pay through the enactment of legislation.		...I hope this information helps &amp; that the #Trumpshutdown doesn‚Äôt last long.		11/11
What is the impact on food safety activities?		The FDA is unable to support the majority of its food safety activities. 	10/11
What is the impact on medical research &amp; the CDC?		NIH shuts down most medical research &amp; the CDC has to stop flu season monitoring, as well as treatment &amp; prevention recommendations. 	9/11
What is the impact on federal housing loans?		The Federal Housing Administration stops approving applications for housing loans. 	8/11
What is the impact on small businesses?		The shutdown halts federal loans to small businesses.	7/11
What is the impact on US military personnel?		The Defense Department says, ‚ÄúMilitary personnel on active duty, including reserve component personnel on federal active duty, will continue to report for duty and carry out assigned duties.‚Äù 	6/11
What is the impact on veterans‚Äô services?		All VA medical facilities &amp; clinics remain fully operational. However, VA call centers &amp; Veterans Benefits Admin public contact services are not available.	5/11
Will I still be able to visit the national parks and monuments?		During the 2013 shutdown, national parks, monuments &amp; Smithsonian museums were closed. The Trump Admin said it will work to keep national parks ‚Äúas accessible as possible.‚Äù	4/11
Will my mail still arrive?		Yes. The ~500,000 Postal Service employees are exempt from a furlough because the Postal Service is self-funded.	3/11
Will I continue to receive my Social Security &amp; SSI checks?		Yes. You‚Äôll continue to receive Social Security &amp; SSI checks. However, new Social Security cards will not be issued.	2/11
